nouvelle scène electro nourrie à soundcloud et aux free downloads. \n\nPuisant sa force aussi bien dans la Future Bass et le Hip Hop que dans la Techno ou l’Electro, cette nouvelle génération de producteurs est le fer de lance d'un mouvement dont le seul mot d’ordre est la création de nouvelles vibes musicales à travers le mélange des genres. Un temple de l’exploration musicale ou l’échange des univers règne en maître.\n\nAu programme de cette première édition, à la Maroquinerie le samedi 1er novembre 2014,\n6 producteurs de la scène internationale en pleine ascension :\n\n\n• GANZ – (NL / HW&W Recordings)\n\nSigné sur le même label que Kaytranada, Ta-Ku ou encore Stwo, l’amsterdamois est l’un des producteurs les plus remarqués sur la scène Bass hollandaise.\n\nhttps://soundcloud.com/iamganz\n\n\n• EPROM – (USA / Rwina Records)\n\nProducteur atypique et novateur, l’américain s’est illustré brillamment au sein de la scène trap et dubstep lui permettant de sortir des EPs sur Warp, Surefire ou encore Bad Acid.\n\nhttps://soundcloud.com/eprom\n\n\n• AAZAR – (FR / Point Point) & LH4L – (FR / Point Point)\n\nIls seront deux à représenter le crew français Point Point :\nAazar, reconnu pour ses morceaux sortis sur Mad Decent et sa collaboration avec ︻ ƱZ ︻ pour \"Shake\", et L’homme aux 4 lettres, porté quant à lui sur la future bass.\n\nhttps://soundcloud.com/whosaazar\nhttps://soundcloud.com/lh4l\n\n\n• MADAME – (FR / Boys Noize Records)\n\nJeune producteur techno originaire de Caen, Madame a su attirer rapidement l’attention des pontes de la scène électronique internationale : Diplo, Digitalism, Crookers, et se produire sur plusieurs spots d’envergure comme les dernières Transmusicales de Rennes.\n\nhttps://soundcloud.com/madamedj\n\n\n• GUESTARACH – (FR)\n\nVeritable oiseau de nuit, résident et programmateur au Social Club, GUESTARACH parcours les scènes et clubs de tous horizons. EPROM is one of the vibrant West-Coast scene’s most colourful characters and an important cog in the international Rwina machine. He&#39;s a consummate post-snake person producer, and his sound varies from toxic hip-hop to searing garage mutations to bizarre concoctions somewhere in between. He&#39;s had releases on Warp, Surefire, and Bristol-based Bad Acid, but it&#39;s his Rwina releases that have been the most visible and enduring, whether it&#39;s the timestretch torture and fierce melodic geysers of &quot;Humanoid&quot; or deconstructionist mayhem of his &quot;Pipe Dream&quot; EP, where dubstep and grime collide for a staggering beast that shakes off heavy blotches of radioactive fluorescent sludge with every beat that lands. His live sets are something to behold as well, emphasizing the hip-hop roots that lurk underneath his sewer beats, and an hour of EPROM is bound to turn your brain into to the same sort of goo that gums the gears of his distinctive beats.Fans and supporters of Eprom include&nbsp;Flying Lotus,&nbsp;Questlove,&nbsp;DJ Shadow,&nbsp;Rustie,&nbsp;THE GASLAMP KILLER,&nbsp;The Glitch Mob&nbsp;and BBC Radio One&#39;s&nbsp;Mary Anne Hobbs, and the producer has shared the stage with many of the international electronic music community&#39;s hottest artists. With his new album, Metahuman, garnering critical acclaim from all corners, Eprom is finally getting the recognition he has earned as an integral part of the giant bouncing backbone of West Coast Camp Questionmark, DJ Dials & 1015 Folsom presents\r\nSHADES + IVY LAB  TSURUDA\r\n+++Soundpieces & Stamina SF Residents+++ BOGL SUBMORPHICS  ADEPT SIKKIE D MAJIK\r\nThursday March 9th / 10pm - 3am / 21+\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nSHADES \r\nFacebook \r\nAlix Perez (Belgium/UK) and Eprom (USA) (Alix Depauw and Alexander Dennis respectively) are SHADES. Alix and Eprom are bass and dance music stalwarts, who have grown to become some of the more influential artists amongst their peers today.   Their debut self titled EP (released on Alpha Pup) is a truly unique body of work. The 85 bpm onslaught is perfect for multiple genres of DJ’s. It is a hard bass driven musical anomaly that is so different, yet fits in perfectly. XLR8R have rightly said “music that's not only a legitimate full-frontal assault in the same vein as tunes from that golden era of gluttonous bass and synths, but that embraces that ethos while giving it a more polished feel”.   Their Second EP “Powers of Two’, was an immediate success, and saw them being booked for shows globally. SHADES toured Europe, Australia and New Zealand in 2015. They are currently on tour in the United States and Canada, and their music has been championed by all of their own biggest influences including The Gaslamp Killer and Amon Tobin. Their third and highly anticipated EP is due for release on September 2nd 2016 on Alix Perez’ personal and highly acclaimed imprint, 1985 Music. The new material is a testament testament to their ethos for progression. It is a hard, dynamic and forward thinking music that works at home, or on a system. It is testament to their maturity and innate progressive attitude toward music.  They have toured Australia, New Zealand, the whole of Europe, Canada, and also the United States several times already since their very recent conception. They are about to embark on another tour of the US, having only just recently finished one. Watch this space.\r\n\r\nSHADES (EPROM X ALIX PEREZ) - LIVE ON UKF\r\nPlays: 28,842\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nIVY LAB \r\nFacebook  Twitter  Soundcloud\r\nNorth London trio Ivy Lab were brought together out of a shared enthusiasm for experimentations on the fringes of the Drum'n'Bass scene. Several years on from that initial coming together, the collective go from strength to strength; propagating a new generation of sub-genres housed within the framework of their '20/20' project.  The middle of the noughties saw collective-elder Gove Kidao build up a sustained presence as a Producer/DJ operating under the name Sabre, working on disparate interpretations of the drum and bass genre for labels ranging from Renegade Hardware to Metalheadz to Darkestral. In 2009 Critical Music served not only as the home for Sabre's debut long player, but also the debut track from an unknown young talent advocated by Sabre to the label. J Fogel a.k.a Stray enjoyed broad acclaim for his inaugural release \"Timbre\", and began to work on further projects for Critical Music, including collaborating with Sabre himself. Unknown to them both, each had independently struck up a relationship with another emerging talent operating under the moniker Halogenix. Collaborating as separate duos soon expanded into combining into a formal trio, casting the foundations of the collective that exists today.\r\n\r\nIvy Lab + Sabre - Oblique\r\nPlays: 446,296\r\n\r\nTickets: After purchasing a ticket through Eventbrite, you will receive an email with your tickets attached as a PDF.
